<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">if</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;(file.exists())&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">if</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;(file.isDirectory())&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">throw</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;</span><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">new</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;IOException(</span><span class="string" style="color:red; margin:0px; padding:0px">&quot;File&nbsp;'&quot;</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&#43;&nbsp;file&nbsp;&#43;&nbsp;</span><span class="string" style="color:red; margin:0px; padding:0px">&quot;'&nbsp;exists&nbsp;but&nbsp;is&nbsp;adirectory&quot;</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">if</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;(file.canRead()&nbsp;==&nbsp;</span><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">false</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">)&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">throw</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;</span><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">new</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;IOException(</span><span class="string" style="color:red; margin:0px; padding:0px">&quot;File&nbsp;'&quot;</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&#43;&nbsp;file&nbsp;&#43;&nbsp;</span><span class="string" style="color:red; margin:0px; padding:0px">&quot;'&nbsp;cannot&nbsp;be&nbsp;read&quot;</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">else</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">throw</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;newFileNotFoundException(</span><span class="string" style="color:red; margin:0px; padding:0px">&quot;File&nbsp;'&quot;</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&#43;&nbsp;file&nbsp;&#43;&nbsp;</span><span class="string" style="color:red; margin:0px; padding:0px">&quot;'&nbsp;does&nbsp;notexist&quot;</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">return</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;</span><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">new</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;FileInputStream(file);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li></ol>

<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px">
&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px">
根据指定的文件获取一个新的文件输出流：openOutputStream (File file)</p>

<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">else</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">

<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;File&nbsp;parent&nbsp;=&nbsp;file.getParentFile();&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">

<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">if</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;(parent&nbsp;!=&nbsp;</span><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">null</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&amp;&amp;parent.exists()&nbsp;==&nbsp;</span><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">false</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">)&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">

<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">if</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;(parent.mkdirs()&nbsp;==</span><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">false</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">)&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">

<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px">
字节转换成直观带单位的&#20540;（包括单位GB，MB，KB或字节）byteCountToDisplaySize(long size)</p>

<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">for</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;(File&nbsp;file&nbsp;:&nbsp;found)&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">if</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;(file.isDirectory())&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;innerListFiles(files,file,&nbsp;filter);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">

<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">else</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;files.add(file);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">

<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li></ol>

<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px">

</p>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px">

<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px">
判断两个文件是否相等contentEquals(Filefile1, File file2)</p>
<div class="dp-highlighter bg_java" style="font-family:Monaco,'DejaVu Sans Mono','Bitstream Vera Sans Mono',Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; width:679px; overflow:auto; margin-left:9px; padding:1px; word-break:break-all; word-wrap:break-word; background-color:transparent">
<div class="bar" style="padding-left:45px">
<div class="tools" style="padding:3px 8px 10px 10px; margin:0px; color:silver; font-weight:bold; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); border-left-width:3px; border-left-style:solid; background-color:rgb(248,248,248)">
<strong>[java]</strong>&nbsp;<a target="_blank" class="ViewSource" title="view plain" href="http://blog.csdn.net/gao36951/article/details/38302553" style="color:rgb(160,160,160); text-decoration:none; margin:0px 10px 0px 0px; font-size:9px; padding:0px">view plain</a><a target="_blank" class="CopyToClipboard" title="copy" href="http://blog.csdn.net/gao36951/article/details/38302553" style="color:rgb(160,160,160); text-decoration:none; margin:0px 10px 0px 0px; font-size:9px; padding:0px">copy</a><a target="_blank" class="PrintSource" title="print" href="http://blog.csdn.net/gao36951/article/details/38302553" style="color:rgb(160,160,160); text-decoration:none; margin:0px 10px 0px 0px; font-size:9px; padding:0px">print</a><a target="_blank" class="About" title="?" href="http://blog.csdn.net/gao36951/article/details/38302553" style="color:rgb(160,160,160); text-decoration:none; margin:0px 10px 0px 0px; font-size:9px; padding:0px">?</a>
<div style="width:22px; height:11px"></div>
</div>
</div>
<ol class="dp-j" style="font-size:1em; line-height:1.4em; margin:0px 0px 1px 45px; padding:0px; border:1px solid rgb(209,215,220); color:rgb(92,92,92)">
<li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px"><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">public</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;</span><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">static</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;</span><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">boolean</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;contentEquals(File&nbsp;file1,&nbsp;File&nbsp;file2)&nbsp;</span><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">throws</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;IOException&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">boolean</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;file1Exists&nbsp;=file1.exists();&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">if</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;(file1Exists&nbsp;!=&nbsp;file2.exists())&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">return</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;</span><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">false</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">

<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;IOUtils.closeQuietly(input1);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">

<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px">
对一个Url字符串进行将指定的URL按照RFC 3986进行转换decodeUrl(Stringurl)</p>

<div style="width:22px; height:11px"></div>
</div>

<ol class="dp-j" style="font-size:1em; line-height:1.4em; margin:0px 0px 1px 45px; padding:0px; border:1px solid rgb(209,215,220); color:rgb(92,92,92)">

<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">if</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;(url&nbsp;!=&nbsp;</span><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">null</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&amp;&amp;url.indexOf(</span><span class="string" style="color:red; margin:0px; padding:0px">'%'</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">)&nbsp;&gt;=&nbsp;</span><span class="number" style="color:rgb(192,0,0); margin:0px; padding:0px">0</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">)&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">int</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;n&nbsp;=&nbsp;url.length();&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">

<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">return</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;decoded;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li></ol>

<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px">
将一个URL数组转化成一个文件数组toFiles(URL[] urls)</p>

<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px">
将一个文件数组转化成一个URL数组toURLs(File[] files)</p>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px">
&nbsp;</p>
<div class="dp-highlighter bg_java" style="font-family:Monaco,'DejaVu Sans Mono','Bitstream Vera Sans Mono',Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; width:679px; overflow:auto; margin-left:9px; padding:1px; word-break:break-all; word-wrap:break-word; background-color:transparent">
<div class="bar" style="padding-left:45px">
<div class="tools" style="padding:3px 8px 10px 10px; margin:0px; color:silver; font-weight:bold; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); border-left-width:3px; border-left-style:solid; background-color:rgb(248,248,248)">

<ol class="dp-j" style="font-size:1em; line-height:1.4em; margin:0px 0px 1px 45px; padding:0px; border:1px solid rgb(209,215,220); color:rgb(92,92,92)">
<li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px"><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">public</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;</span><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">static</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;URL[]&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;toURLs(File[]&nbsp;files)</span><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">throws</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;IOException&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;URL[]&nbsp;urls&nbsp;=&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">new</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;URL[files.length];&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">for</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;(</span><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">int</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;i&nbsp;=&nbsp;</span><span class="number" style="color:rgb(192,0,0); margin:0px; padding:0px">0</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">;&nbsp;i&nbsp;&lt;&nbsp;urls.length;i&#43;&#43;)&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;urls[i]&nbsp;=files[i].toURI().toURL();&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">return</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;urls;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li></ol>

拷贝一个文件到指定的目录文件并且设置是否更新文件的最近修改时间copyFileToDirectory(File srcFile, File destDir, booleanpreserveFileDate)</p>
<div class="dp-highlighter bg_java" style="font-family:Monaco,'DejaVu Sans Mono','Bitstream Vera Sans Mono',Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; width:679px; overflow:auto; margin-left:9px; padding:1px; word-break:break-all; word-wrap:break-word; background-color:transparent">
<div class="bar" style="padding-left:45px">
<div class="tools" style="padding:3px 8px 10px 10px; margin:0px; color:silver; font-weight:bold; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); border-left-width:3px; border-left-style:solid; background-color:rgb(248,248,248)">

<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">if</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;(destDir&nbsp;==&nbsp;</span><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">null</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">)&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">throw</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;</span><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">new</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;NullPointerException(</span><span class="string" style="color:red; margin:0px; padding:0px">&quot;Destination&nbsp;must&nbsp;not&nbsp;be&nbsp;null&quot;</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">if</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;(destDir.exists()&nbsp;&amp;&amp;destDir.isDirectory()&nbsp;==&nbsp;</span><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">false</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">)&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">throw</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;</span><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">new</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;IllegalArgumentException(</span><span class="string" style="color:red; margin:0px; padding:0px">&quot;Destination&nbsp;'&quot;</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&#43;&nbsp;destDir&nbsp;&#43;&nbsp;</span><span class="string" style="color:red; margin:0px; padding:0px">&quot;'&nbsp;is&nbsp;not&nbsp;adirectory&quot;</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;File&nbsp;destFile&nbsp;=&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">new</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;File(destDir,srcFile.getName());&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;copyFile(srcFile,&nbsp;destFile,preserveFileDate);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li></ol>
</div>

<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">if</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;(srcFile.exists()&nbsp;==&nbsp;</span><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">false</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">)&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">throw</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;</span><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">new</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;FileNotFoundException(</span><span class="string" style="color:red; margin:0px; padding:0px">&quot;Source&nbsp;'&quot;</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&#43;&nbsp;srcFile&nbsp;&#43;&nbsp;</span><span class="string" style="color:red; margin:0px; padding:0px">&quot;'&nbsp;does&nbsp;notexist&quot;</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">if</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;(srcFile.isDirectory())&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">throw</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;</span><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">new</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;IOException(</span><span class="string" style="color:red; margin:0px; padding:0px">&quot;Source&nbsp;'&quot;</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&#43;&nbsp;srcFile&nbsp;&#43;&nbsp;</span><span class="string" style="color:red; margin:0px; padding:0px">&quot;'&nbsp;exists&nbsp;but&nbsp;is&nbsp;adirectory&quot;</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">if</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">(srcFile.getCanonicalPath().equals(destFile.getCanonicalPath()))&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">throw</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;</span><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">new</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;IOException(</span><span class="string" style="color:red; margin:0px; padding:0px">&quot;Source&nbsp;'&quot;</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&#43;&nbsp;srcFile&nbsp;&#43;&nbsp;</span><span class="string" style="color:red; margin:0px; padding:0px">&quot;'&nbsp;and&nbsp;destination&nbsp;'&quot;</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&#43;destFile&nbsp;&#43;&nbsp;</span><span class="string" style="color:red; margin:0px; padding:0px">&quot;'&nbsp;are&nbsp;the&nbsp;same&quot;</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">if</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;(destFile.getParentFile()&nbsp;!=&nbsp;</span><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">null</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&amp;&amp;&nbsp;destFile.getParentFile().exists()&nbsp;==&nbsp;</span><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">false</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">)&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">if</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">(destFile.getParentFile().mkdirs()&nbsp;==&nbsp;</span><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">false</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">)&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">throw</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;</span><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">new</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;IOException(</span><span class="string" style="color:red; margin:0px; padding:0px">&quot;Destination&nbsp;'&quot;</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&#43;&nbsp;destFile&nbsp;&#43;&nbsp;</span><span class="string" style="color:red; margin:0px; padding:0px">&quot;'&nbsp;directory&nbsp;cannot&nbsp;becreated&quot;</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">if</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;(destFile.exists()&nbsp;&amp;&amp;destFile.canWrite()&nbsp;==&nbsp;</span><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">false</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">)&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">throw</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;</span><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">new</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;IOException(</span><span class="string" style="color:red; margin:0px; padding:0px">&quot;Destination&nbsp;'&quot;</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&#43;&nbsp;destFile&nbsp;&#43;&nbsp;</span><span class="string" style="color:red; margin:0px; padding:0px">&quot;'&nbsp;exists&nbsp;but&nbsp;isread-only&quot;</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">

<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">

<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;doCopyFile(srcFile,&nbsp;destFile,preserveFileDate);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">

</p>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px">
拷贝文件到新的文件中并且设置是否保存最近修改时间doCopyFile(File srcFile, File destFile, boolean preserveFileDate)</p>

<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">if</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;(srcDir.isDirectory()&nbsp;==&nbsp;</span><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">false</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">){&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">

<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">throw</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;</span><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">new</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;IOException(</span><span class="string" style="color:red; margin:0px; padding:0px">&quot;Source&nbsp;'&quot;</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&#43;&nbsp;srcDir&nbsp;&#43;&nbsp;</span><span class="string" style="color:red; margin:0px; padding:0px">&quot;'&nbsp;exists&nbsp;but&nbsp;is&nbsp;not&nbsp;adirectory&quot;</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">if</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">(srcDir.getCanonicalPath().equals(destDir.getCanonicalPath()))&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">

<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">

<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="comment" style="color:rgb(0,130,0); padding:0px; margin:0px; width:auto; border:0px">//&nbsp;Cater&nbsp;for&nbsp;destination&nbsp;being&nbsp;directorywithin&nbsp;the&nbsp;source&nbsp;directory&nbsp;(see&nbsp;IO-141)</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">

<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;List&lt;String&gt;&nbsp;exclusionList&nbsp;=<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">null</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">

<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">if</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">(destDir.getCanonicalPath().startsWith(srcDir.getCanonicalPath()))&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">

<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">if</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;(srcFiles&nbsp;!=&nbsp;</span><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">null</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&amp;&amp;srcFiles.length&nbsp;&gt;&nbsp;</span><span class="number" style="color:rgb(192,0,0); margin:0px; padding:0px">0</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">)&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">

<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;exclusionList&nbsp;=&nbsp;newArrayList&lt;String&gt;(srcFiles.length);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">

<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}&nbsp;<span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">else</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;doCopyFile(file,copiedFile,&nbsp;preserveFileDate);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">

<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="comment" style="color:rgb(0,130,0); padding:0px; margin:0px; width:auto; border:0px">//&nbsp;Do&nbsp;this&nbsp;last,&nbsp;as&nbsp;the&nbsp;above&nbsp;hasprobably&nbsp;affected&nbsp;directory&nbsp;metadata</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">

<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px">
copyURLToFile(URLsource, File destination, int connectionTimeout, int readTimeout)</p>

<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px"><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">public</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;</span><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">static</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;</span><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">void</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;copyURLToFile(URL&nbsp;source,&nbsp;File&nbsp;destination,</span><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">int</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;connectionTimeout,&nbsp;</span><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">int</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;readTimeout)</span><span class="keyword" style="color:blue; font-weight:bold; margin:0px; padding:0px">throws</span><span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;IOException&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;URLConnection&nbsp;connection&nbsp;=source.openConnection();&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;connection.setConnectTimeout(connectionTimeout);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">

<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">

<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;copyInputStreamToFile(input,destination);&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; color:rgb(85,85,85); background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">
<span style="color:black; margin:0px; padding:0px">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></li><li class="alt" style="font-size:1em; margin:0px; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border-left-width:3px; border-style:none none none solid; border-left-color:rgb(153,153,153); line-height:18px; background-color:rgb(245,250,226)">

</p>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px">
拷贝一个字节流到一个文件中，如果这个文件不存在则新创建一个，存在的话将被重写进内容copyInputStreamToFile(InputStream source, File destination)</p>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px">
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
